O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	You, three heads of the son, I have fulfilled this book that is behind the science of medicine the fulfillment of it, and have finished for its exposures and by its declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And I have seen come to me in vision that I have completed this with this cauterization, which is from the work of hands, it is to know "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is forbidden in our region and is disfigured in every way, if it is perceived by the science and obscure, and there is nothing more to do than the small descriptions in the books of the ancients that the hands have moved.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And from this comes the error and emptiness, and the intentions are closed and science is alienated.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation; et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	It seems to me that I would bring it back to life by assembling the order of this cauterization according to the way of exposure and declaration and abbreviation; and I will assemble the forms of the knives for cauterization and other tools of the work with the alignment of the declaration and preparation of it, as it is their craft.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And because no skilled hands masters are found in our time, the art of medicine is elongated.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And it is necessary for him who enters this to surpass in the science of anatomy, as Galen says, so that he knows the judgment of bones, and their forms and conjunctions and separations of parts, and have knowledge of bones, nerves, and limbs and the number of joints, and the movement and rest of the legs, and also of their issue.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc; et meismement en l’art de main.	And for this reason, Iphicas says that the non with the non is not enough, and with the hand it is little; and at the same time in the art of the hand.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes; ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	In the introduction of this book, we say that those who are not acquainted with these things are in error and do not understand men; therefore, I have often seen many who enter into this science and abandon it and its experiment.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col; por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	For I see a mad man who cuts off the head of an abscess or the neck of a woman, and cuts the arteries of the neck; because so much blood issues out that the woman dies in his hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans; si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	And see if another mirror that treats a piercing of a man's ear, and the piercing was large; if it is carried with it a piece of the bladder, and died the man in three days.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	I have already been accused of the practice, and see the position of the patient and the size of the piercing, and if it was well that it was cut, then it died.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie; et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine; et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie; et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	And see if another mirror that cured the duke of our land who had a broken leg, and with the fracture caused a wound; and the patients were ignorant and forced the fracture on the wound as soon as possible, and did not leave any pain in the wound, and eventually finished it; and he commanded that he not slip; and later, when the leg was completely swollen and the bone and came to destruction.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe; et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	I am called to come to him, and I hurried to come remove the leg; and when I dislocate it if it is not in pain and does not feel any pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner; et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	But all the way the corruption was confirmed or member, and could not be healed; and the corruption continued to spread through the member as long as the member was completely wasted.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And see another wonder that will fall and enchantment, and then inflame by the evil of his lordship.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For chancre, when it is free of melancholic matter, only then does it happen that if one touches it with iron, it will not be able to do anything else than what is corrupted.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions: c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions; et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	And for this reason, three times, I advise you that the work of hands is divided into two divisions: it is knowledge, whether it is harmful in other dispositions; and I will show in each page of this book where there is fear and danger.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez; et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit; et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	If you do not keep yourself informed, they may speak ill of you. Take your weapons carefully and lightly, but firmly, and use the best way possible for the grace of God to save you and be healthy; and leave unwholesome diseases behind you; and keep your weapons from doing evil, and be sure in yourself that you can come from this world to another with glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens: «Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	Galen's advises in his advice: "Do not take unwholesome remedies for your sicknesses, lest you become more wretched.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have seen this treatise according to three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez; et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	The first chapter is about fire cauteries and medicinal cauteries, and it is ordered from the head down to the feet; as well as the forms of strangulations, and of burns with cauteries, and of all that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses; et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	The second chapter is about cutting and pricking, and ventouses and wounds, and the extraction of arrows, and similar things; and it is ordered and the forms of strangulations.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses; et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	The third chapter is about restoring dislocations and twists, and similar things; and it is ordered by the main doctor's experience, and the forms of the stitches.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	However, if we remember the work, it is necessary that I give the quality of the help and not every complexion.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus; et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu; et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	I say that the quality of the help, and not every complexion, is the longest word and subtle science and the secret remedy; and for this they speak more of the wounds, and agree to it, and few words are said because I doubt the longevity.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions: c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	I say that cauterization helps universally with all types of matter, as long as the matter is present: it is to know hot matter with matter, and dry matter with matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide; et li autre dirent le contraire: que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	In hot and dry matter, no one will prescribe it and say that cauterization is great help; the other says the opposite: that cauterization is only good for diseases that come from choler and sweating.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour; et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	For the nature of fire is hot, and should not be cured by hot disease from choler, nor by sweating; and those who say the opposite that cauterization helps greatly with hot diseases that come from men's courage.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	For as soon as you perceive the chest of the patient and its moisture at the complexion of hot fire, you must quickly close the chest.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree with this word.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have never found it at any time by experience.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens; des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	And every way, it does not interfere with anything but those who have experienced it and know by long practice the chapter of cauteries, and the diversity of complexions in men, and their dispositions and causes of their diseases, and their symptoms and spasms; other complexions have no fear, even in cold and moist diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	The patient should assemble and align with the fire cautery.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	Understand, children, that the fire cautery assembles when it has secretions of remedies, and even more benefit than the cautery of burning medicine.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For the flesh is simple, and only causes harm to the member that is cooked, and does not harm other members.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation; et par aventure ocit lou malaide Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	The burning remedies come from one member to another by allaying, and bring the maladies of grief to health; and by chance often lo the patient the flesh for its highness and for the benefit of its substance does not cause harm, if it has superfluity.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses; et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant; or le recevez en vos pensees.	1. And I found this in my research through experiment and the length of service and the study I have dedicated to the art, and it is true about things; and for this I apologize for the length of the language, as I only want to share with you the secret that is inside or fire, and the quality of the work, as it treats the maladies of the body, just as the philosopher says by demonstration; and receive it in your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	2. And know, son, that the cauteries should be made in such a way that they fit well, and they should be prepared.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere; et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	3. And I say that cauterization is acceptable in all cases, because the wounds are not misplaced by the help of the cauterization; and moreover, if the cauterization is for necessary pain and hastates that cannot wait for the time that greatest malice does not come to the member.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire; car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue; et il le dient ensi; mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	The patient should never think that the wound is healed just because it has been burned; for the disease that is cured by cauterization has no return; and they tell him so, but it is not always true, because cauterization is only a medicine that dries up the complexion and drys the humors that cause the pain, and is as good as any other medicine to hasten one's valor, and for the virtue of one's work and nobility.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut; et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie; mais ce avient poc.	However, there are times when the disease returns according to the complexion of the patient and the weakness of their illness and virtue; and they assemble upon them the superfluities through the acquisition of meat and such things, unless cauterization is given to them or they have little superfluity and moisture, like cauterization for the pain, and the symptoms, and the part of the pain returns but seldom. However, this is rare.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir; mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	And many people do not understand why cauterization is called the "end" of medicine, but it is to see; but they only believe that cauterization is after medicine, but we understand that it is before medicine because when we administer remedies for any disease and they are ineffective, then we use cauterization and it works.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	Therefore, it is well said that cauterization is the end of medicine, not according to the attention of the gullible.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance; et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes; et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	The ancients said that a gold cauterization instrument was as dangerous as iron, and they said this was due to the quality of the gold and the high content of its substance; and they said that the gold cauterization instrument does not cause any harm, but it is not true to see, and I have experienced it myself and found that it is true in some people; and gold cauterization is as good as iron, as they say.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez; et s’on le chaufe trop; si font au feu; et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	When you hold the gold instrument, you do not know how much it is heated by its gold color and how much it has cooled down; and if you heat it too much, it will melt in the fire; and then it will be enough to prevent it.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And that's why we use our fire cautery because we have not managed to complete our work.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or you have ordered this chapter of the lighter bones, because it is easier to find.
dou cautere olivaire	oil cautery
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	This cauterization is used for moisture and coldness in the head, and it is done due to a disease called "soda", and due to many humors that descend from the head to the ears, eyes, and jaw, as well as numerous dreams and pain in the throat and chest, and even for all diseases that come from coldness such as paralysis, apoplexy, and seizures, and similar diseases.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir; et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	The form of this cauterization is if the patient is purged by solvent medicine altering the head III nuis or IIII, according to which virtue and age and custom of the patient he can endure; and then make the head of the patient.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis; aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz; et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	And then place the root of your palm between the root of his nails on his two fingers; and if you come to your two hands, if blood oozes out, then wash the cauterization which is called "olivare", of which the form is:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant; puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit; et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit; aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors; aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre; et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	And then place it on the knee sign of ink, and make descending and pulling your hand a little by a little until you see the bone I small; and if you do not see it, then the cauterization resumes as long as you see the bone as I have told you; then take the point of the needle, and put on soft cotton dens, and place on the knee, and leave it III jors; then make on the wound with moistened gauze; until the burn is dry; then cure the wound with the ointment called "tetrafarmaçon" as long as it is healthy.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge; et por ce si aide mues.	And they say to the elder, that the more overturned the wound is, the more it discharges; and for this reason it helps to alleviate.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And none of these say that the fire cautery should be so harsh as to take part of the bone, and then remove what is burned from the bone, and treat it.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors; et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte; aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	And they say that the fire cautery should be so harsh as to burn through, and push so hard that it breaks the bone just as wide as the vertebra that women put in their fuses because the humors exit outside; and then it should be left overturned for a long time; after that, it should be treated and closed.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor; et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier; car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres; et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	1. These two methods of cauterization do not seem to be the best in total, whether for men or women who fear; and I think it is better to leave them; because the head of the patient is weakened by continuous natural solutions, as we have experienced in other parts; and even when the patient's strength is weak naturally, the first appearance of cauterization seems more salving and milder to me, and I perform it therefore with care.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	2. of the ancient pain of the head
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres; et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	3. When the entire head is afflicted with chronic pain that lasts long, and it must be treated with the patient's own herbs and pills called "cochies," and purging of the head and oils and plasters; and when the cauterization is done as we have described before, and it does not help.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit; adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	The patient's condition is severe, and it should not be too cold; therefore, we cauterize the area with the fire cautery as we have described earlier.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»; et est I leus en coi on met ventouses; et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os: li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors; et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	After cauterizing each corne of the eye, as we have previously described, and then cauterizing the area called "vassels" where the veins are located; and they are placed with a ventouse. And hold your hand so you do not see the bone: the patient feels too much pain in this cauterization than in others, and I will explain further; and it is necessary that the cauterizations of the corneas be more subtle than those of the veins, and this form is:
dou cautere dou chief	For the fire cautery, instruct the patient to let the hairs grow long and
Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie: adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	When sudden pain occurs in one part of the body, and it spreads to the whole body, and the head is purged with medicines, and the other treatments I have mentioned in the division of diseases are made, and none of them benefit: therefore, I made the cauterizations in two ways, that is, with hot medicine and with iron.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir; et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres; et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III; puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	If you apply a poultice of alum to the wound and scar, and then cover the head with the pouch containing the doses of alum, and then remove the dose of alum from the curd; and when it is removed, if the patient holds the dose of alum well and leaves it on for twelve hours; and then remove the dose of alum and apply a poultice of sulfur, and leave the wound for two to three days; and then put the pouch back on the wound as soon as possible.
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	After the cure of ointment as it is healthy; and if you see if I make any such remedies as I have written or treat of remedies for remedies.
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	The fire cautery if it follows this method.
Chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	Heat the cautery of copper, and its form is:
Et est apelez «clos» por ceu que li chief est fait a la forme d’un clo ou il ait I poc de corbeure, et em mileu a une petite apparance; et le met sor le leu dolorous, et tien ta main et trestorne le feir un poc legierement, tant que li moitiez de l’espés dou keur soit arse; et lieve ta main que li artere n’arde, que est defuers, et decorre habundance de sanc.	And is called "closed" because the head is made in the shape of a cage or has an opening, and looks small; and it is placed on the painful part, and hold the patient's hand and gently press the iron on the half of the curve as much as the pain allows; and ease your hand that the artery does not burn, which is gentle, and causes abundance of blood.

After sewing with linen thread, and then put the limb for three days; then he puts linen cloth in the bure, and then treats the limb with ointment until it is healthy; and if you want to cauterize this wound with the cautery called "cultellare" at all points, and keep away from the artery in this wound that is not near.
de emigraine	of the wound
Quant tu cures emigraine si com nos avons devant dit en divisions des maladies, et ne profite mie, et vois que li cauteres devant dis de la medicine et dou fer ne li soffit mie, adonques covient il que tu eschaufes le cautere qui est apelez «cultellare» tant qu’il soit blans; et seigne ainsois sor le leu doillant une ligne de demi doi de lonc, et oste ta main une fois, et l’estrain que tu ne coper l’artere et que ne viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde de la mandibule que muet quant on menjut, et li ners n’ait regart que la muet et que spasmus ne veigne a malaide, et te warde de decorrement de sanc de l’artere quant elle sera copee, ou copement ait grant paour et meismement a celui que ne s’i conoit, et qui n’est estudians et esprovez; et laisse l’uevre em mi voie; mais je vos dirai coment on restainche sanc quant li artere est copee, et je vos mostrerai a leu ou il afiert en cest livre.	When you treat the wound as we have said in divisions of diseases, and do not profit, and see that the cauterization before does not help, then it is necessary that you use the cautery called "cultellare" as much as possible; then mark a line of half a diameter on the limb, and with your hand once, and draw it so that you do not cut the artery and do not pull it too hard on the bone; and you will need the mandible that is silent when it is cut, and the nerves only have silence and spasmus when they are cut, and you will need decorrement of sanc from the artery when it is cut, or cut with great pain and immediately to the one who does not know it, and who is not studied and experienced; and leave the wound in its place; but I will tell you how to relieve pain when the artery is cut, and I will show you where the artery is treated in this book.

de la cure de fistule par cautere	Translation: "Of the cure of fistula by cauterization
Quant tu cures fistule si com nos avons dit en divisions des maladies, et tes cures ne profitent mie, adonques covient il que tu li fais cautere selonc ceste maniere. After that, form the cautery as described, and hold your hand on the cautery at the part where it is not greasy with oil, so that your hands do not slip; then place the cautery in the oil-greased part, and it will corrode.
Se tu viens au comencement dou cautere jusc’a l’os, si serait bien.	If you come to the beginning of the cautery before the bone, it would be better.
Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors; aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers; et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	If not, then restart the cautery again and if you are able to do it again, leave it for three days; after that, put cotton wool in the burette, and apply the desiccating ointment as long as it is dry, and when 40 hours have passed, if it is still dry, then apply an acidic corrosive medicine as long as the bone is exposed; and follow according to what comes in your chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And there is a way of cauterizing fistulas that no ancient ones mentioned.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu; aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	Under the fistula, and open the leg; then put in the forceps of the subtle cord that is its form:
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc; et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil; et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe: li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	And they make it to the quantity of a .З. of plaster; and hold your hand on the forceps firmly, and do not move the patient's limbs at all, only the plaster will stick to the oil; and it is necessary to put the oil on the smooth cotton cloth in the navel or in the wound: the plaster if it adheres well to the fistula, and the patient's skin becomes healthy.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	If the fistula is healed by the fire cautery we have described, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	If not, then administer the purging of the belly and return the fistula to its proper place according to what is best for the patient's own belly.
des crevaices en levres	gums in the mouth
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Gums in the mouth sometimes come and are called "hair," and also in the mouths of children.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these gums as we have described in divisions, and the cure does not benefit, then use a small fire cautery according to this form:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font; aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And he puts it in those fissures as much as possible; after curing the limb with salve until it is healthy.
de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess of the gall
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule; et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie: adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule; aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu; et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez; et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	When an abscess forms in the gallbladder or uterus, or ovary, or roots of teeth, and it becomes inflamed and turns into a fistule; and you cure it as we have said in divisions, and it does not profit: therefore, it is necessary that you cauterize according to the size of the fistule; after the blotch or purulence of the fistule, and hold your hand until the fire escapes from the wound, and if it does not come out; and once or twice, after curing what we have said in the cures, as soon as it is healthy; and if it is cured once or twice, that is good; and if not, then you must expose the limb and open the corrupt bone, according to what you will find in your chapter.
dou movement des dens	The first sentence to translate is "Ou cautere de
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain; aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent; et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent; aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit; aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	When the gums are softened by moisture and the teeth move, and you treat them with medicines and it does not work, then put a piece of wet cloth in your mouth; afterwards rinse the cautery that came from this part in the same way as you place a nail in a tooth; and pull out the teeth with the cautery, and hold your hand tightly so that the patient feels the pain coming from the root of the tooth; afterwards gently release your hand and continue the cautery according to your will; afterwards fill the patient's mouth with wet earth, and paint it once a day and keep it fresh.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	And in a similar manner, if the teeth that were moving are confirmed, and the gum is softened and restrained, and the moisture is dried out and becomes dry.
de la dolor des dens	of the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres: et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	When the pain of the teeth comes from coldness, or if it is cold or visible, and the remedies of medicine do not work, then it is necessary to have a cauterization done in two ways: cauterization with brimstone and cauterization with fire.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain; aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez; et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	Cauterization with brimstone if it is such that you prefer brimstone of wool, and the end in a iron or brass cup; then take cotton and wrap around the point of a pin, and make it with brimstone built, and place it on the painful tooth firmly and hold until it becomes cold; and often I do this as long as the virtue is alive at the root of the tooth, and if you see that the wool and cotton are burned in brimstone, and place it on the tooth with fire as much as the flesh reaches to the end of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide; aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez; fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	1. The fire cautery is applied when it is hot enough to burn a piece of iron or silver, and it should be large enough that the fire does not reach the mouth of the patient; afterwards, touch the cautery with your hand, and place it on the tooth, and hold your hand there until the cautery is cool; do this often, as the pain will be less for you or the next day.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	2. It is necessary that the patient fills their mouth with a piece of cloth in the pressure of this cautery, and then releases it; and this is the form of the cautery:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir; et c’est li forme de la caine:	And make a burn as hot as you desire, according to what you can bear; and this is the shape of the candle:
des scrophules	And then make a scar from the burn, according to
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie; et met le cautere chaut sus l’apostume une fois, ou II se mestier est, tant qu’il viegne au font de l’apostume; et se li apostume est petis si met cautere selonc la quantiteit de l’apostume, et le laisse ensi III jors; et met sus coton moilliet em burre tant que li arsure soit ostee; aprés cure le leu d’oignemens et de tentes tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when the burns are soft and cold, and do not respond to digestion with medicines, then wash the burned area with water, and after the form comes out, make an opening for the smoke to escape from the other side; and put the candle on top of the abscess once, or as it may be, until it pours out of the abscess; and if the abscess is small, put the candle according to the amount of the abscess, and leave it for three days; and cover the wound with moistened cloth as much as it hurts; afterwards cure the lesion with ointments and poultices as much as it is healthy.
Li forme de la cainne:	The form of the chain:
Quant les moistors vainquent sus les chenals dou pormon, et meismement quant ce vient de froide complexion, adonc covient que li malaides soit voidiez premiers par medicines solutives; aprés li fai cautere a la racine de la gorge, et te garde que tu ne venir mie jusc’a la gorge, et n’ardre dou keur mais c’un poc.	When the moistors win over the throat's opening, and immediately when it comes from cold complexion, then the patient must be first treated with soluble medicines; after that, I perform a fire cautery at the base of the chin, and make sure you do not go too far into the chin, and only burn a little bit, not too much.
Aprés li fai I autre cautere a la jointure dou col au chief de l’espinee, et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» de coi nos avons la forme devant; et cure le leu si com nos avons devant dit tant qu’il soit sanez.	After that, I perform another cautery at the joint of the shoulder blade and the head of the spine, and it is called the "clavicle"; and treat the limb as we have said, as long as it is healthy.
de la toust	Of the entire
Quant tous et maladie de pormon sont de moistors froides, et li malaides nen ait fievre ne sechor, et est li maladie anciaine, se li fai ij cauteres sus la forcele en leus vuis; et I autre cautere emmi le pis entre II mameles; et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» selonc la forme qui est devant dite.	When all the symptoms of porrigo are due to cold moisture, and the patient has no fever or chills, and it is an acute disease, then make two cauterizations on the sides; and the other cauterization is made between the second and third molars; and this is called the "clavicle" according to its form as mentioned earlier.
Et se tu vues, fai cautere en poignant a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins» de coi li forme est ci devant en la maladie des oreilles; et soient li poins jusc’a XXX, ou enqui entor.	And if you see, make cauterization by pricking at all the cauterizations called "points" in the form of the disease in the ears; and let the points be as close to 30 as possible, or at least one on each side.

de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the dislocation of the shoulder
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.

et cauterize lou keur tant qu’il le perce jusc’a costeit, et venrait li fugure dou cautere ensamble IIII cauteres; et por ceu est faite cautere avec le cautere qui a III ners, por coi li figure de cauterization sunt sis cauteres; et sont li nerf selonc la subtiliteit d’une tente et c’est li forme dou cautere qui a III ners:	And cauterize the wound as much as it pierces the cost, and it would come out with four cauters; and this is made with the cautery that has three needles, because the figure of cauterization is six cauters; and these needles are according to the subtlety of a tent and it is the form of the cautery that has three needles:
Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce I nerf por coi il i a VIII cauteres.	And never has it been adjusted on this wound because it has eight cauters:
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil; aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	After, put the cautery on the wound with a needle; after, let the patient rest, and do not press on the limbs as long as they are well comforted:
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	If it is dislocated again, something comes out quickly, therefore make a cauterization on the large cauterization clavicle, or on the point of cauterization when pricking.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	Because the joint is closed, and it is healed by the moisture and is healthy for the patient.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When the stomach comes with coldness and moisture as it is drawn to its complexion, and the catarrh is multiplied on it, and the usual cures are applied, and it does not benefit, then the patient must have the physician's care on his back, extend his legs and hands.
De ceu en aprés li fai III cauteres I desoz la cuillier dou pis per la quantiteit d’un doi, a tout le cautere clavile, et II cauteres defuers les II costez tant que li figure des cauteres soit a III angles, et ait teil espaice entre l’une et l’autre qu’elles ne soient jointes ensamble quant elles giteront porriture; et soient li cautere si parfont qu’il porpreignent les II pars dou keur, et soit li figure des cauteres selonc ceste forme sens ajostement:	1. For the third time, I made three burns on the thigh of the patient with the quantity of one drop, at all the cauterization points, and two cauterizations on the costal cartilages so that the cauterizations are at three angles, and there should be space between them as they will produce sweat when they grow hair; and they should be like this so that they do not touch each other when they sweat:
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme; et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche; puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	When you see a large cauterization on the stomach according to this form; and the one who has fear of this cauterization, cauterizes by pricking and holds by the stomach and not according to the quantity that you see of enche; then the cauterization covers the entire cauterization that is called "points".
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the cure of the cure we had before, as long as it is healthy.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez; et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil; et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient; et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi; et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere; et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez; et s’il ne peut, si soit gisans, et estende ses jambes, et lieve ses brais; et c’est li forme:	When the liver has pain from fever and moisture and great viscosity, as long as it is placed in its natural complexion due to superfluities; and the patient is cured according to what we have said in divisions, and it does not benefit him if he becomes sick due to his hatred; and a sign of enche III cauterization according to this form and figure and quantity on the liver, defeat the hypochondriacs, either from the stomach or from the belly comes; and there should be space between each cautery of a grown-up man's limb; and they should not press too hard with their hand on the cauterization; and so only half of the moisture should be applied, and the patient should be dry on his knees; and if it cannot be done, then it should be extended with his legs, and he should lie down on his back; and this is the form:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors; et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	If you wish, if you cauterize these sharp cautery points, be subtle and gentle in your craft, and make sure you do not burn the entire body, as you would dry out the whole body; and that it does not become muddy, as the hair is very delicate in certain places, and you want to see.
Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile: s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort; et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee.	When it has gone into the liver, and you see whether it is in the liver or not: if it is in the liver, it feels the pain of the cauterant but not too much; and if it is on the skin, it feels sharp pain.
Et lors quant ceste cure desoit les mires, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus sa teste; et puis seigne d’enche le leu ou li apostumes est, et puis chaufe le cautere qui est semblans au rais, de coi ci est li forme:	When this treatment of the burns is completed, if the patient's skin is not swollen on their face; then stretch the skin where it is swollen, and then heat the cauterization tool that resembles a rake, according to what is appropriate.
Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers; aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez; et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois.	And cauterize the area as much as the skin is burned, and it becomes white, until the flesh is completely charred; after the treatment according to the treatment of wounds as long as it is healthy; and it is only necessary to use this cauterization tool with no other tools than those who have studied for a long time in the art of medicine, and by their hands these diseases have never been corrupted once.
Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	Therefore, it is difficult to overcome, and I seem that it is better to leave it alone.
dou cautere de pleuresin	Do not cry, the cauterization will help.
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere: pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois; et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe; et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc; et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules; et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	The ancients said that one must make cauterization with roots of Aristolochia, and in this way: take a long root of Aristolochia as you can find, dry it, and make it as large and long as your two thumbs; then put it in oil, and heat it until it is hot enough to cauterize. Cauterize between the forceps and the collar, and two punches in descending order in the part that is loose at the beard; cauterize between the fifth costal cartilage and the seventh rib, declining downwards on one punch; cauterize the pituitary gland, and the other in the stomach, and the two shoulder blades, and the pits defend the cautery that is between the shoulder blades; do not press too hard with your hand, as you would smell.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme; et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	And no ancient said that no man uses fire cauterization like the raser, and they thrust it and put it between the ribs, as soon as it comes to the abscess; and then there is the pain, as we have said in the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this case, there is pain or the patient dies now, or fistula comes that cannot be healed.
de la mice	of the mouse.
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of the mouse that we have said in the divisions of the cures, and it does not profit much, therefore there are three ways of cauterization that you all know.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant; et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos; et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule; et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	1. de ydropisie	of dropsy.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not for dropsy, but in the way that is called "ascites".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur. Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere; et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	After the patient has been cauterized with a long, thin piece of fat, and does not bother the physician after the cauterization; then the cure will be quick, and they will be assembled together with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit; et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	The form of the cauterization is made in the belly, either with the rib that we show before it; and on the back, it is made like an elbow, according to what is placed before it.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the enflaming of the wounds
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	When the wounds are inflamed with hydration, and they are plain greenish, it is necessary to cauterize on the back of the wound between the auricle and the anus; and gently hold the cauterization with your hand so as not to turn.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too much in front, otherwise the wound will become infected, and let the cauterization be done according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire; et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe; et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse; aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	Afterwards, make two cauterizations on each leg at the point of the nail; and let the cauterization be long, one before the genital area and the other after, in the leg; and leave the cauterizations to heal for a long time, until the wound is cured; afterwards, cure the other cures that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the menstruation
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures; et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule; et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	When the abdomen is cold and moist, as long as the digestive and absorptive virtues in the stomach and intestines are swollen and inflamed, and cannot be cured by usual means; and you see the patient suffering greatly and with weak constitution, then make a large cauterization at the stomach according to what has been spoken of before or at the stomach; and four cauterizations are made around the bowels subtly, and two cauterizations are made on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	If you see many moisture and the patient is suffering, then the fire cautery should be performed on the point where it hurts, and on each side of it, and on the large part of the stomach, because the cure is effective when it has good help.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the cure of the hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres: III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois; et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile; et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	If the hemorrhoids are deep-seated, or one or more, and are old and large, and consist of cold, moist, corrupt humors, and are treated as I have said in divisions, and if it does not profit, then perform cauterization: III on the spine of the back, which is completely raw and cut into small pieces, and the cauterization on the anus II doses; and if you think that the stomach is cold and the meat is not cooked, and you see the face swell, then the face on the large cauterization on the stomach, as I have said earlier, and the liver and gallbladder on one side, and the other on the other side; leave the cauterization over long.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After healing the limb as much as possible.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the chalcedony which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit; et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort; fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit; aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez; et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	When you heat the chalcedony, if it appears to be the cautery, and then place it all flamed on top of the heated chalcedony; and leave as much of your hand as the cauterization reaches to the vein's birth, without cutting; do this once or twice, and if you have no more chalcedony, then cauterize each time as we have said; after the cure of wounds as much as possible; and if you cauterize with a larger cautery on a heated iron, it will give more help.
de plaie mal curee	A wound that has been improperly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot endure tightening or opening, we will tell you about it in their own words, if they come to a disease that cannot be healed because of cauterization.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	If no fistula comes, and it is awake and exudes milk and corrupt moisture, if you prove it to be totally silent, and keep hold of all the tent until it has enough.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing; et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	After scraping the cauterization that seems to be the rasping, and cutting it in the fistula according to the quantity that enters, and then reapplying the cauterization as much as the corners and edges are corroded and crushed; once, or twice, depending on the amount of fat that is present, and large wounds.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans; aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement; et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font; et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	1. If the fistula would be in the course of the ureter and intestine, if one were to perform these loops, and only do this in the gut, and think that it is not a serious matter; afterwards cure the belly as much as it is healthy, and if the loop is removed, and the materials are long bones, then it is certain that the belly is entirely healthy; and if the materials are long bones, then it is certain that the belly is entirely healthy, and if the materials are not long bones, then it is certain that the belly is corrupted in its foundation.
de la maladie des reins	2. of the disease of the kidneys

de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce; et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing; et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	When the bladder is full and weak from headache and moisture, if the patient retains urine, then you should cauterize the urethra at the part where it enters the bladder, either on the left or right side, and do so in each place as one would on a penis; and you also cauterize the back of the urethra, or two more; and the cauterizations should be done according to the form mentioned before.
de la marris	Of the marsh
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde; et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor: adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos; et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.
