de la hainche	Of the heel
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble; et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle; et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	When the viscous moisture descends to the heel of the foot, and for this reason if it does not move from its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when measured together; and it is found that the knees are in a different department wanted, then it comes that you should cauterize the patient's shoulder above the heel of the foot in the manner of a circle, and follow the shin forward around the heel until the heel turns, so that the heel is within the circle; and if it is the cauterization such as those made on the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs; et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If this cauterization is not present, make three large olive-tree cauterizations and they should be as sharp as all the thorns; and the cure will be safe once it is healed.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the gallbladder
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene: adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	When pain comes in the gallbladder, and it is cold and moist, and the patient is treated as we have said in the division, and the cure is not effective, and the disease is old: then it is necessary to purge the patient of large amounts of fetid pills or other bone-like pills.
Aprés li fai cautere; et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres: c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	After the cauterization: and the manner of cauterization is as follows: it is to know how to assemble burning medicines and cauterize with fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz: que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire; aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	For the fire cautery, if it is done according to methods, then some are like this: you cauterize on the handle of the thorn III cauteres triangularly according to this form, and make good depth and great width, and it should be between every cauterization of an inch the growth of a tooth, and it is olive oil; never done once on the tip of the thorn, for it has four like this form.
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche; mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you see, if the cauterization is done at the circular cautery we mentioned in the dislocation of the thorn; but make it in a part way that the circles contain the entire thorn, and all the points as they are.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way it is done in sciatica, when the pain holds in the hip, and does not reach the thigh or the knee.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc; et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur; et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	And when the pain comes to the thigh and the knee, if the patient feels the pain there, and the surgeon says that the pain is in this area, then cauterize the heel four times, on the side nearest the little toe; and if it is a cauterizing burn, and if the patient feels that the pain spreads to two points or close by, then cauterize where the patient feels the pain three or four points on the cautery which is called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus; et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	And if the pain is from the knee to the thigh, then cauterize with a circular or cutting cautery; and be careful in all your cauterizations that you do not burn the nerves and large arteries, and that you cause less harm and contraction to the patient.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	I have also seen others who cauterized on the ankle and caused so much pain that the entire leg became swollen, the foot, and it was noticed and corrupted in all the toes.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a solution of belly which caused death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	If the pain is in two parts assembled, make a fire cautery on both sides according to this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce; et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait; et c’est li forme:	And the woman said in the fire cautery of the thigh, according to this manner, make I such iron and so at the head either as big as some nail's tip or a smaller one, and so by interlacing and so are between each other in spice the quantity of a new of peas; and they be the interlacings of II parts, and they also like noses, and have I the handle of well-made iron; and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit; et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors; et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens; aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	1. And let it be shaved as much as it is all red and glistening, and then put it on the handle of the male cauterizing iron, and make it bend once to the cautery reign; and then apply some ointment, and leave the wound open for three days; and then cover it with a plaster, and let the wound heal completely.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent; et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	1. Albucasim says that we use little of this cautery because of its fear of the cold, and if we use it a little, all these cauteries can be endured; and all this is about the cauteries that can be endured, whether they are hot or cold.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi; et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	The first line of the text translates to: "If you have a burn cauterization instrument and you descend it along the edge of the door, and it is made of iron or steel with a long point, and in the upper part, there should be two of us, and one between each quantity of a doe; they should be overturned and cut off, and they should join together according to this form:".
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche; aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After putting the burning stick on the patient's shoulder, gently press your hand on the stick; after, let it remain between the two circles of hot water that is heated in the fire pot, and leave it for an hour, and suffer the patient's pain and the burn and the soreness of it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu; et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit; et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait; et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	For the burn is as if by fire; and when the burn has passed, ease your hand with the instrument and raise the hot stick of water, and leave it for three hours, and take baths as long as the blackness of the burn is not healed; and then take three hours of the bath as soon as the wound is clean; and this will help after the cure of wounds as long as it is healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument; et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	1. If the pain spreads to the thigh or leg, make an instrument that matches the size of the wound you made in the shoulder; and this is the way to heat the tool, and I have written or described the method for correcting the medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	1. Mix alkali and live fire, as much of one as the other, and blend them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir; et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main; et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	1. If there is a small hole that can be pointed with a razor and entered, and then pour the contents of one pot into another well-mixed pot, and add alkali and salt and gentle heat until you have enough powder to touch with your hand; and leave it until it drips with water or can be poured, then take all of this, and mix it with salt and alkali as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	When it comes to treating fever, one should use remedies from the field of medicine and cauterization on other parts of the body. For she makes a work like fire, and if other medicines are well cauterized, such as those made with henna, anacardium, and chalk with soap, all these things mixed together will help.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	Galiens tells us of a remedy that was used to treat the pain of the scalp and sciatica, and he says that this is the only cure, and that it was cured in one session every time this remedy was applied, and he was bathed as instructed after the treatment.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie; et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	And then in another way, you should rub the patient's limbs with fresh and dry dough, and grease them with a little grease, and put it on the shoulder, thigh, and leg where the pain is, and leave it for three hours and according to the amount that the patient no longer feels the pressure.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	Then I put him in a bath as much as his chest is raised, and then I let him enter the water, and the pain will leave completely and he will be cured.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And you should advise that no one should use such a hot cauterization medicine after the evacuation of blood.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout; et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	When the science of the vein is cauterized with the hair of a goat, if it helps, then it must be made in part this way.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take the gall and grind it with oil, then put it in the flask that is between the little finger and the other which is called the fozen.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains; et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee; et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	After the hair of the goat is dry, and put it on fire until it is charred, and then put on the wool, and leave it as long as it is stained; and repeat again, and continue to do so as you think that it will reach the bone, and that the pain is gone; and this way of cauterization is called "cauterization with goat hair.
de la dolor dou dos	From the pain of the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, whether by touch or percussion or from too great evacuation, or from the appearance of expanded cold matter, none of these appearances is worth cauterization, but rather for that which comes from the infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir; et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»; et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	It is necessary after the patient has been purged of fetid pills or other substances, that you cauterize on the back of the patient, where the pain remains, three lines marked with a lancet, and in each line V cauterization or more according to the skill and quantity that the patient can bear; and make the cauterization according to the cautery called "points"; and if you see, make III cauterizations or IIII on the clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor; et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	Many times this disease comes to children as small signs, and the signs of the beginning are that they become stiff when they wake up, and fear; and you see the spines of our backs and the appearance that comes with the other spines.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you see it cured, if the cauterization is done at the fire according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	If the cauterization penetrates every part of the spine evenly.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see, if the cauterization is done at the end of the spine by pricking two or three lines, and they are points close to each other.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After the limb is healed according to what we have said, and you are warned that you will not perform a fire cauterization on the spine that is in the nerve.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When the pain of the joints is due to moisture that has expanded to every part of the body, and when the pain comes in the foot, which they call "gout" properly, and when it is of a cold cause and remedies by medicines do not cure, then it is cured by cauterization in this way: make a cut around the joint of the foot, and the cauterization should be olive-shaped according to this form.
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	If it is your desire that you prick the cheek with a sharp point, then the cauterization is done throughout the entire cauterization as claimed "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if the pain comes to the knee and other joints, and this happens many times, then the cauterization is done on each knee III or IV of each part, throughout the entire olive-wood cauterization; and if you have more skill, but do not hold your hand as long as the pain allows.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pain descends to the knee and to the back, apply the cauterization that we have described in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	And if the pain remains in the hands, I make points on the flesh of the second line; and if there is no more pain, I make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand; and if the pain comes from the elbows or shoulders, I cauterize each part and give the patient medicine and government to the physician.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you give him medicine and purge the poison, he will be saved by God's help.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the face.
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When rupture comes in writhings, and the blood descends as streams and it is new, if it comes to your curing before it pains you, it will not be able to come back; and it should use things that relieve the stomach, if it comes down from the stomach; then make it sit on its back between your hands, and command it to lick its tail as soon as it is repaired, and tie it with your fingers to your two thumbs, and sign to close the rupture on the bone of the affected limb, and make a sign that resembles half a circle around the whole; then wash the cauterization with the form you have:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as it is white and glistening, feel it.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then smooth the wounds on your legs; and the surgeon will cleanse his hands so that they do not get dirty; and well work on the thighs with the patient, and put the cautery sign on all of your hand, and hold it correctly and firmly until you reach the bone, and if you don't reach it the first time, then repeat it again as you go until you touch the bone; and be careful that the blood does not come out while you are making the cautery, that you do not burn it; and so that the patient does not die or suffer from other wounds.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And you should know that when you do not come to the bone at the cauterization, your efforts are in vain.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	It is necessary that the cauterization of children be subtle according to the measure of the bone, and also great for adults; after three days, cure the wound of the cauterization as much as possible until the burning is healed; after the cure of other ointments as long as it is healthy, and make the patient lie on his back for forty days until the wound is well sutured; and it is necessary that the stitches be tightened for a long time, so that the blisters do not come out when they are raised in the chambers.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	After forty years, when he wishes to rise, he will find a well-made scar on his neck, and after thirty more years; and he should rest, so that he can work quickly and avoid excessive intoxication with drink and drugs, and excessive yawning; and when he teaches this lesson, it is entirely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say this after the trimming in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupturing of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures occur in other abdomens and are known, and you see that they are not increasing, if you re-cauterize according to the quantity, and so is the third angle according to this form; after the treatment as we have said; and no of the ancients has said that it should be cauterized at three angles according to this form.
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	1. The shoulder is dislocated and I make a line for the width of the fracture, and another for the defense, and hold your hand to all the cauterized clavicle.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	1. However, the first cauterizations are more gentle and less painful.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	1. there is no pain in any limb.
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	1. When pain comes to any part of the body, whether from cold or injury, and this pain lasts for a long time, and medicine does not help, then it is necessary to cauterize at the cauterization that is called "points", and the cauterization should be according to the length of the limb and its narrowness and sharpness and its knot and its location of knots and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the first cauterization is healthy, it's well; if not, restart another cauterization on the same member, because it is customary for the patient to die at the member that is proximate, since it is necessary to perform the cauterizations until the patient becomes healthy.
de meselerie	of miscarriage
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	Miscarriages are never helped by cauterization once, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of flesh and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	Can you see the cauterization, take care when the disease is at its beginning, and cure according to what we said in the division, and do not stop or delay, and you doubt that corruption will spoil all the patient, therefore I perform the cauterizations on the head: I cut off the head, and the other towards the front at the end of the wounds; and I sew the two corners, and the heel to the hip; and it holds so much of your hand that the cauterization sticks to the bone, and as long as the discharges issue forth so that the vapors of the large humors may issue forth; and cauterize the nose according to what is before you.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	1. If the healing process is widespread; it is evident, if you cauterize the wound with these cauters we have mentioned or chief, and the cauters in general, and the cauters at the point of the shoulder, and the cauters at the point of the back, and the crupie and the other delez, and theII sus the II espaules; and theII sus the tendrons dou pis, and theII sus each joint of the hands and the feet, and the fosses of the hands; and you have nerves that are below the shoulder calcining, which you do not burn; and never made a cauter on the bone of the elbow, and the other on the stomach, and the other on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	When more fire cautery is done, the patient receives more help and benefits from it; and you should know that the patient does not feel pain in the fire cautery as much as they should, because the heart is already somewhat corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it should be that the fire cautery is large and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in the ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After treating the dough with flour and honey, and other remedies, as long as it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the member is infected and treated with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healthy, then the fire cautery is done on the member according to its size and thickness; and the cure of ointments as long as it is healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	And never has it been done to cauterize and at the hand, foot, and back, at the end of the nerve that is silent on the member, and if it is not enflamed; and none will interfere unless they know the members and the movements of the nerves in the body.
de albaras	of barbers
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "albaras" is awakened, and the art of medicine does not help, then it is cauterized with a cautery one point at a time, according to the amount of the vessel's swelling, as long as the blister is not enflamed, and is not green in color; then the cure of flour and lentils with olive oil and plantain flakes, and sage and almond, of each part; and all assembled are moistened, and dressed with a linen cloth, and applied to the body as it becomes healthy.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of syphilis by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the sore first appears, and you see it stop, if the cauterization is done at the cauterization point that seems to be a circle, all around the circumference of the sore.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And the wise say that cauterization is done in the environment of the sore; and I do not see any other way, because I doubt that it will not become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already wanted this to happen once; and the most correct thing is that it be cauterized around, at the cauterization point that is called "circling", as we have said in our mouth about cauterization.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the flesh that cannot be cut
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When someone has a disease called 'adubelati', and it delays in dying either due to excessive excretion or lack of blood when the patient is old (i.e., too many) and has little strength, or for other reasons; and you see it struggling to die: therefore, the cauterization is done by making small incisions with cauters as they are pinched; afterwards, it is left alone.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will try to die.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it struggling to die, if the cautery is hot enough, then it is the form of the cautery that causes it.
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	When the patient has the disease called "adubelati" as long as the cauterization is perceived by the cur, and such cauterization that the patient feels it in a way that the course of the urine is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the cure, when it is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	the cure by fire with iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another type of disease is called "corrodens", and it is nothing but a rot of the member, because it eats the members as it does the dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the member that can suffer cauterization with fire, then sharpen the cauterizations clavile as small and great as necessary, according to where the disease is; after cauterizing all parts as much as possible, so there is nothing left of it, that all that is corrupted is osteit.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	Then let it remain for three days, and put on the burned parts with oil until the scars from the hot iron are healed and all the corruption is cured.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of burns caused by fire.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if after three days no healthy char is born, it is good; and if it does, continue the cauterization on the parts that are corrupting.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this is never been treated with medicine applied to the cauterization of fire; but all cauterization with fire is greater help, and I have already said the treatment of the medicine ague in division: take the amount you have skill in.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of porings that come to the toe
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	often happens that the toe is affected by a disease called "closed" according to our understanding, and it is a large thing that causes pain in the toe.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the treatment of this disease is done in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is to know that the treatment is by fire cauterization, and by hot iron cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is done by heating the iron as hot as a burning stick, and it is made of a thin piece of iron according to the size of the nail, and it is made as large as possible so that it can cover the head of all nails, and it has subtle margins; then it is placed on top of the nail, and turns your hand around the nail until it reaches the end of the nail; and it leaves for three days until it starts to ooze pus; then a poultice of boiled mugwort is made with salt, and it is placed on the toe all night, and the nail will come out of its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wound with ointment as soon as it is healthy.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	If the wound becomes infected many times in the hand and fingers, and it converts to burning heat; and it is done like this: take an iron nail or a copper wire, or a feather, and put on the nail or the wire and the cloth, it is known to cover warts; and then put the nail on so that it covers everything, then put a spoonful of hot water, and hold your hand well, and press your hand as you turn until the edge of the nail reaches the root of the cloth, and then find the hot water way smoothly at the root; and endure the pain of the hot water for a little while; then let it go, and it will all fall off at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	I then make another after, as you are raising all these that are in the course, and cure the wounds that entangle hair.
li cure dou trembler	I cure it to stop trembling.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	If any tremble from cold or fever, or other, if it is necessary that you make four cauters or four on the back, one between each spike; and one between the stomach and the olive cauter; if it stops the trembling, and when it gets better, the health improves from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of pimples that have appeared.
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No time is seen by defuers the body's skin, or pustles that come from large corrupt materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is necessary to cauterize as soon as they appear, which is a subtle cautery of martyre's wax, or if the point is seized by fire, or from the root of Aristolochia long, or with the lenticular cautery.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And no time is cauterization done at the beginning when they appear, according to this manner, and they do not grow new shoots in front, but are disfigured by the superfluity that comes, and are healthy; but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is tied off
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Many times there are great hemorrhages of blood from the artery that is tied off at the wound that comes at the pardefuers, or at the incision of the abscess, or at the fire cautery of the member, and similar things; and it is a very unfortunate thing to have to open the vein.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And when there is none, if you have to put your index finger in the wound of the vein, and hold it as tightly as possible until your finger is numb and no longer hurts; then heat the olive oil cauters more often and larger until they are all red; then I, or as much or as little as needed, open the wound and lay the artery in front of you, and put the cautery on the vein where you have your finger, and hold the cautery as tightly as possible until your finger is no longer sensitive.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	If it happens that you feel your child's vein when you prick it with the cautery, and the cautery has stopped, then quickly take another cautery that is hot.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And do not stop doing this one after the other until the nerve is no longer tender; and be careful that you do not damage the flesh which is sensitive, and that no other malice comes to the patient's side; and advise that when without cutting the artery, one cannot well restitch immediately when the artery is large, it is not by cauterization or extraction if it is not properly treated, nor by too tight a thread, nor by medicines put on which have the power to cause pain, but by tying and drawing tight.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever will manage the tightening of the knots or the placement of burning things on, or other similar things, should not profit from it if he does not have time.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines. If you see the wound, if no drop of violet or thread oil is distilled, then extraction is performed; I make the patient lie down, and they sneeze as they extract, and their nose is covered with pieces of linen or wool; and the ear is covered.
Mout de fois vient fuer par ceste cure; et s’elle ne vient fuer, se li amenistre extraction as pinceures subtilz, de coi ci est li forme:	This treatment is often used; and if it does not work, then the patient is subjected to extraction with fine tweezers, and the form is as follows:
S’elle saut fuer as pinceures, c’est boin; se ceu non, si amenistre extraction a l’oncine subtil de petite doubleure; et s’elle ne saut par ceu, si fai une caine d’arain et boute lou chief de la cainne ou pertuis de l’oreille fort, et estoupe ceu qui est entor la cainne de cire mole si que li vens n’i puisse entrer avec la cainne; puis le trai fuer forment, car mout de fois vient fuer si com nos avons dit; et s’elle ne vient fuer en teil maniere, si prent glut de coi en prent les oisiaus, et met en som aucun estrument qui soit a point por ceu faire, et met un poc de coton entor; puis presse le glut sus la piere ou quel chose que ce soit, et trai fuer.	If it jumps with the tweezers, it is good; if not, then extraction is performed with fine tweezers of small double loop; and if it does not jump with this, then I make a gauze suture and cut the tip of the gauze and push the end through the ear hole, and cover the part that goes through the ear wax so that it cannot enter with the gauze; then the treatment is formed, as it comes often as we have said; and if it does not come in this way, then take a little glue on the fingers, and put any instrument that is not sharp enough to do this, and put a piece of cotton inside; then press the glue on the wound or whatever it is, and suture.
Et s’elle ne saut fuer de toutes ces choses que nos avons dit, si te haste de fendre l’oreille ainsois que aposteme chalz i veigne, et spasme; et li maniere de la fendure si est que tu faices premier sainier lou malaide de la cephalique, et estrai dou sanc selonc la mesure de sa vertu, puis fai seoir lou malaide entre tes mains et li torne l’oreille au desus, et fent une petite fendure en la racine de l’oreille a la graisse ou leu dependant; et soit li fendure ausi com une lune, tant que tu viegnes a la piere, puis l’oste selonc ton pooir, et la suce hastanment a ta bouche; et la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	If she does not jump from all these things that we have said, and you still have the ear open but in pain, and the spasm; and the way of the ear fencing if it is that you first clean the patient's head of the cephalic chalzy, and then draw out the blood according to its strength, then place the patient between your hands and turn the ear towards the side, and make a small incision at the root of the ear in the fat or depending on the lobe; and the fencing should be like a moon, as you go to the piercing, then the bone according to your will, and the suction strongly in your mouth; and the cure as soon as it is healthy.
Et se c’est grains qui est ens et il enfle, si aministre extraction; et si’il ne puet issir, si amenistre I spatumile tenve subtil selonc ceste forme:	And if it is grainy and swells, administer the extraction; and if it cannot be removed, then apply I spatumile subtle according to this form.
et amenistre incision de celui grain.	and make an incision on that grain.
Mais ne faire mie ceu quant tu penses que li grains est moistes por la moistor de l’oreille, tant que tu en aies fait maintes pieces; puis l’estrai as pinceures subtilz et au succier, si com nos avons dit, si que li estractions soit aligie.	But do not make the incision if you think the grain is moist from the ear's moisture until you have made many pieces; then extract it with fine pincers and honey, as we have said, if the extractions are alleviated.
En l’aigue donques que chiet en l’oreille covient que li malaides use d’esternuement de condisi premiers, et ample l’oreille de viel coton.	In the ear, therefore, that the patient has grains in the ear, it is necessary that the surgeon uses the first condiement of the cloth and amplifies the ear with soft cotton.
Et soit gisans sus celle oreille meisme ou li aigue est.	And let there be caution with the same ear or eye.
s’elle saut fuer per ceu, c’est boin.	If she jumps for this reason, it's good.
se ceu non, si prent maintes pieres selonc li longesce de ton doit tenves et legieres, et les eschaufe un poc au feu; et em mette li malaides une ou pertus de son oreille, et saille sus i. de ses piez d’autre part, et fiere d’une autre piere sus la piere qui est en l’oreille; et ne cesse de faire ceu de piere em piere tant que li aigue isse toute fuer, et ensi saut elle toute fuer; et se tu vues, si prent I jonc, et boute l’un des chiés en l’oreille, et l’autre chief emprent de feu tant que li plus dou jonc soit ars; puis refai autreteil d’autres jons tant que li aigue isse toute, si com nos avons dit en la piere.	And if she does not jump, then take several piercings according to the length of your horse's neck and light ones, and burn them a little at the fire; and put the mallet on one ear, and pull out the other part, and cut it off from another hole in the ear; and continue this for each hole until the wound is completely healed, and when she jumps again, if you see that the other ear is also swollen, then take one of the ears and burn the other end, and the other ear will be taken away as hot as possible; then make another part of other holes as long as the horse's neck is completely healed.
En l’estraction de la beste, s’elle est de petit cors, si com puce et semblans chose, cure la si com nos avons dit en la division; mais s’elle est de grant cors c’on la puisse sentir, si amenistre extraction de pinceures; et c’est li chose plus legiere a oster qui soit en l’oreille.	In the extraction of the tooth, if it is small, like a flea and similar, it can be treated as we have said in the division; but if it is large, one can feel it, before the removal of the forceps; and that is the lighter thing to handle, which is in the ear.
En l’estraction des vers enjanrez as oreilles, quant tu lou cures si com nos avons dit en la division et ou traitier des distillations, et li cure ne profite mie, si covient que tu regardes l’oreille au soleil: s’il i apert nulz vers, si les trai as pinceures subtilz, et s’il n’aperent, si prent la cainne de coi ci est li forme:	In the extraction of the ears, if you treat it as we have said in the division and after treating with distillations, and the cure does not profit much, if you look at the ear to the sun: if there are no holes, if you take subtle forceps, and if there are, if you take the cat's grip of this form:
Et soit estroite desoz et large desus.	And let it be narrow and wide.
Et boute lou plus subtil chief en l’oreille selonc la quantiteit de la soffrance dou malaide, puis succe forment a tot la caine; fai ceu sovent tant que tuit li ver issent.	And bite deeper in the ear according to the amount of suffering the patient endures, then continue until the wound is completely healed; do this often as often as necessary.
Et s’il n’obeissent a issir, si estoupe entor la cainne de coton si com j’ai dit en la piere; et s’il ne saillent fuer si com nos avons dit, si aministre distillations que li ancien ont esprovees en l’ocision des vers, et tu les troveras ou traitier des distillations; et si distille tes oiles et tes medicines en l’oreille a tout cest estrument, de coi ci est li forme si com tu vois:	And if they do not heal, if the wound closes over the cotton glove as I have said in the incision; and if they do not come out as we have described in the decision of the verse, and you will find them or treated with distillations; and if you distill your oils and medicines in the ear using this instrument, whatever form it may be, then:
Et soit d’argent ou d’arain estrois desoz a I petis pertuis, et desus overs por distiller; et por presser dedens la distillation a I estrument d’arain bien fait por ceu, et se tu vues pren I raseur et envoloupe entor la pointe avenanment coton; puis i giete ton oile ou ton jus, et ceu que tu vues de tes medicines en la cainne, et li caine soit en l’oreille; puis boute dedens lou raseur a tout lou coton, et presse ta main tempreement tant que li oile soit distilleit ou chevement de l’oreille; et lou sente li malaides dedens, et soit li distillations I poc eschaufee au feu ainsois c’on la distille en l’oreille; et garde qu’elle ne soit trop froide, car li medicine ne seroit mie si bone.	1. Then, if gold or silver is mixed with the ointment, and it is rubbed in; and to press the mixture into the well-made copper instrument, and if you see take the rasor and envelop around the point of the needle; then it will glide your oil or juice, and what you see of your medicines in the case, and the case is in the ear; then dip the rasor into all the cotton, and press your hand firmly until the oil is distilled or comes from the ear; and it will feel the patient's pain, and so the distillations I poc eschaufee at the fire are also done in the ear; and keep it not too cold, for the medicine will not be good if it is.
de l’estoupement des oreilles	Of the fever of the ears
Aucun enfant naissent qui n’ont nul pertus ens oreilles; et ceste meisme chose avient as homes par estoupement de plaie, ou de char nee dedens l’oreille, et cist estoupemens vient aucune fois em parfont en l’oreille, si c’on ne lou puet veoir; et aucune fois avient I poc defuer lou pertus, et lou voit om bien.	No child is born without some ear infection; and this same thing happens due to fever or trauma to the ear, or a hole in the ear, and there is no sign of an ear infection every time it comes, if one cannot see; and never has there been a deflated ear drum, and it looks well.
Celle donques que vient em parfont, si c’on ne la puet veoir, est de grief sanation em plusors dispositions, et en cele c’on voit covient que tu mettes l’oreille dou malaide au soleil; et regarde dedens: se tu vois l’opilation apparent, si la oevre a tot cest spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	That which comes in front of it, if one cannot see it, is a sign of a slow recovery in other ways, and in this case, it is recommended that you put the ear in warm water; and look: if you see the apparent inflammation, then the ear has totally become this swelling form.
Et soit agus et trenchans devant et derrier tout plain, si qu’il ne blece l’oreille; se li opilation est de char nee ou cors de l’oreille, si la tien as pinceures subtilz, et la cope legierement, tant que celle chars soit toute ostee.	And so, and thoroughly clean both sides, if it does not cause pain; if the exfoliation is of char or cors of the ear, if the hand has subtle pincers, and the glove lightly, as long as that char is entirely removed.
Et se li opilations est em parfont en l’oreille, si pren I raseur subtil legier et l’eschaufe un petit au feu, puis li met ou cors de l’oreille.	And if the exfoliation is fully removed from the ear, if you take a soft gentle rasping tool and slightly heat it, then it puts on either char or cors of the ear.
Se tu sens l’opilation dont li malaides sent grieteit a l’oïr, perce legierement, et garde que tu ne grever les ners de l’oreille; puis met en l’oreille une tente selonc la largesce dou pertus, et la moille en l’oignement egyptien.	If you feel the exfoliation that the patient feels pain in the ear, gently pierce, and be careful not to hurt the ear nerves; then put into the ear a tent according to the large opening of the hole, and apply Egyptian ointment.
Fai ceu aucun jor tant que li plaie soit soudee, ou tu pren une tente et la moille en aigue rose, et poudre sus vitriole broiet; et se tu vois enflee l’oreille, si couvient que tu traies la tente et remue une autre tente moillie en cerote qui soit fait d’oile roset et de cire, tant que li enfleure soit ostee; puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	1. Do nothing until the wound is healed, or take a tent and moisten it with warm rose water, and sprinkle it with powdered vitriol; and if you see blood coming out of the ear, then cover the tent with another soft tent made of olive oil and wax, as long as the discharge is bloody; then apply the cure once it is healed.
Et se decorremens de sanc vient, si plonge une esponge et drapelz en aigue froide, et le met sus l’oreille, et use d’autres cures qui oste lou decorrement de sanc qui sont ou traitier des destillations.	2. If the discharge of blood increases, then dip a sponge and wet it with cold water, and place it in the ear, and use other remedies that stop the flow of blood, which are treated with distillations.
de la char des papieres	Of the scroll of paper
Cist althelul que vienent em papieres des eulz quant ils sont moiste et sont sec, si covient que tu les estendes de tenailles et de pinceures, et le cope d’un spatumile de ses racines; puis met sor le leu vitriole broiet.	That is the head that comes on paper when the hairs are moist and dry, if you stretch them with needles and tweezers, and then place it on a spatula of its roots; then put the lew in vitreous broth.
Et se sans en decort, si le cauterize dou cautere lenticulaire subtil, et li cauterizeir aprés l’incision vaut mues; et maintes fois repairent, cant aucune chose demoure de lor racines; et quant elles sont cauterizees par feu, si sont arses celles racines et ne revienent mie.	And if it is not decorticated, then the fire cautery subtle cautery will be sufficient, and the cauterizer after the incision is enough; and they are always repaired, no matter what happens to their roots; and when they are burned by fire, their roots are arsed and do not return.
de la gresle	Of the grease
Maintes fois vienent em papieres des eulz unes choses que semblent gresle en sa forme et en sa duresce, et por ceu est ceste maladie apelee «grandine», et est une assemblee de moistor grosse en la papiere desus et desoz; li ovraiges est telz: pren warde se li grandine se muet d’une part et d’autre, et c’est legiere chose a savoir; fent la donques dou large, puis l’escorche de chescune partie legierement, puis la prent as pinceures, et la cope.	Many times, things come in papers that seem greasy in form and hardness, and this is the disease called "granule," and it is an assembly of moisture large in the paper of it and its edges; the treatment is as follows: first, if the granule is still from both sides, and it is light to know; then make it wider, then scrape off each part lightly, then take with tweezers, and close.
se tu ne la pues coper sens percier un poc la papiere, si ne grieve rien au malaide; et se li fendure est grans, si l’assemble a une costure, et la cure tant qu’ele soit sanee; et s’elle est petite, si n’i faire point de force, car li oignemens la restoure tantost et enjanre char.	If you do not feel the paper with your fingers a little, and if it is not hurt the patient; and if the assembly is large, if it is sewn at a stitch, and cure as much as it is healthy; and if it is small, if it does not make force, because the restoration of the other parts is so much and unjust.
Et se li grandine est dessendans au dedens de l’oreille vers la partie desus, si enverse la papiere, et estent la grandine a unes pinceures, et la cope et presse d’une part et d’autre; et se li papiere est esloignie par l’incision, ce ne grieve rien; et quant li grandine est copee, si leive l’oil d’aigue salee, et cure le leu de ceu qui enjanre char tant que li malaides soit sanez.	1. If the ice is descending towards the ear hole, if inverted, the paper will hold the ice with tweezers, and the cloth will press from both sides; and if the paper is removed by incision, it causes no harm; when the ice is pressed, lift the salty oil from the eye, and cure the leu that has been injured as much as the malady is healed.
de la graisse des eulz	2. of the grease of the hairs
Exinach est une graisse qui est enjanree en toiles des papieres desus, et ce avient plus as enfans c’a nules gens, et grieve mout a lor eulz, et li vienent li catharre as matinees, et ne pueent regardeir la lumiere dou soleil por ceu que les larmes se hastent a lor eulz; et por ceu se couchent il sor lor faices adés, et dorment sus, et sont lor papieres desoz lor sorcilz moistes que li enfleure et li apparance ont covert de l’exinach qui apert en l’oil.	3. Exinach is a grease that sticks to the threads of papers, and this happens more often with children, and causes pain to their hairs, and they come to the catharsis in the morning, and cannot see the light of the sun because their tears have reached their hairs; and for this they lie on their faces, and sleep, and are covered with wet papers that the ointment has made glisten with exinach.
Et quant tu presses lou leu a tes dois et sent l’exirnach entr’ous.	When you press on your joint and feel the exertion within it.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige si est que li malaides mette son chief en ton sain; et puis pren I drapeil de lin, et appareille une tente em maniere d’un cercle selonc la quantiteit que conteigne exirnach de chescune partie, puis le met sus li; et presse a tes dois d’une part et d’autre, si que li exirnach soit assemblez emmi le cercle; puis fent em mileu de la moistor au spatumile trenchant une fendure dou large, et ne soit mie plus grans que li plaie c’on fait a la sainie de voinne; et fent le cuir em parfont tant que tu veignes a l’exirnach; et em plusors dispositions vient exirnach de la fendure, selonc la forme d’une piece de graisse blainche.	And the manner of the wound is if the patient places their head in your hand; then take a cloth and make a circle according to the quantity of exertion in each part, and place it over the wound; and press on both sides, so that the exertion is assembled within the circle; then apply moisture to the spatulum, cutting a large groove, no larger than the wound you make at the skin's edge; and then make the cloth as large as the wound appears; and in other positions, exertion comes from the groove, according to the shape of a greasy, white lump.
Estrai la donques a tout une piece de drap charpit entre tes dois au defuer, et torne ta main a destre et a senestre tant qu’il soit espars; et garde que tu n’ajoster en la fendure, que tu ne viegnes a tout le spatumile jusc’a l’oil, que tu ne le bleces.	1. Cut the thread at all pieces of bedclothes between your two arms and turn your hand to the right and left as much as it is possible; and hold that you do not pull on the thread, that you do not touch any part of the body except the oil, that you do not hurt it.
Et se li exirnach n’apert en l’encomencement de la fendure, si acroi un poc la fendure legierement tant qu’il apere; puis l’estrai si com nos avons dit, puis moille drapelz en aisil et en aigue, et met sus le leu, et estrain de bendelz.	2. And if the thread does not open at the beginning of the faring, then lightly open it as soon as it appears; then pull it out as we have said, and then tear the cloth in half and in quarters, and put it on the arm, and bind it tightly.
Et si a de tels homes qui broient seil et mettent sus por corrompre cele moistor qui est demoree.	3. And if such men break their silk and put it on to corrupt the moisture that is dried.
Puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then the cure, as long as he is healthy.
Et s’il vient au leu aposteme chaut, si lou cure d’emplaustres assouajant tant qu’il soit sanez.	And if it comes to the abscess apoplexy, then the cure should apply dressings as long as he is healthy.
des poilz des papieres	of the paper's hairs
Quant em papieres naissent poilz ajostez autre que li naturez, et sont enveillit, si nuisent as eulz, et font venir manieres de maladies si com larmes acostumees et mollifications des papieres et albugine, tant que c’est cause de la destruction des eulz; et est li cure selonc IIII manieres: ou par cautere ensamble feu, ou par medicine ague selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre de cautere, et est fais ou par incision et costure ou par caines, selonc ceu que je dirai.	When paper hairs are grown on paper, and they are woven, if they harm the eyes, and cause diseases such as tears and paper degradation, until it is caused by the loss of hairs; and the cure is done in four ways: either by fire cauterization together, or by medicine according to what is before or in the chapter of cauterization, and it is made by incision and stitching or by needles, according to what I will say.
Il covient que tu mettes lou chief dou malaide en ton sain, puis torne la papiere de l’oil a ta main senestre; s’elle est convertie, c’est boin; se ceu non, si i boute une aguille a tout I fil desus; et soit ce delez la marge de la papiere ou li poil naissent delez ces poilz, et trai I fil au desus a tout la papiere, et la torne au raseur; puis fent en la partie desoz la papiere, desoz les poilz ajostez, a tout le spatumile copant, des le grant larmier jusc’au petit; puis estrai I fil, et met desoz la papiere une petite tente de couton et de drapeil, puis seigne sus la papiere une figure d’enche, si com la fuelle de mirte, et toutevoie il covient que li figure soit selonc la quantiteit que tu vues eslever la papiere qui est devisez a toz.	It is necessary that you place the head of the patient's arm in your mouth, then turn the paper of the thread to your left hand; if it is converted, it is good; if not, then insert an awl into all the threads of the spool; and make the margin of the paper or the hair that grows from these hairs, and roll up the paper in your left hand, then cut off the part at the end of the paper, the hair adjusted, throughout the entire staple, from the largest to the smallest; then draw out the thread, and put a small knot of cotton and silk on the paper after, and sew a figure on the paper as if it were the button of a shirt, and if you see that the figure is according to the quantity that you see rising the paper that is designated to you, then it will be necessary that the figure is according to what you see.
Et si a teil qui a mestier c’on cope grant quantiteit de la papiere selonc ceu que li papiere est mollifie; puis fent a tout le spatumile sus les II lignes que tu as signiet, et comence des lou grant larmier jusc’a petit; et soit li une des fendures pres des poilz naturez en la groissece d’un raiz, puis boute l’oncine en l’un des II angles dou keur, puis l’escorche toute; puis assemble les II levres a une costure d’une aguille a tout I fil de laine subtil, et essue le sanc, et fai aerdre la superfluiteit des filz sus les II sorcilz a tout aucunes choses gluans, se tu vues faire ce; et se ce non, si n’en aies cure, puis laisse la costure et les filz jusc’a III jors ou IIII; puis cure la plaie sens costure de choses sechans et constrignans, car li papiere se relive au soudement de la plaie et l’assemblement de li, mais li costure est muedre (si com dirent li ancien), et c’est ovraiges sens paor; et si a une autre maniere: et est que tu seignes la papiere d’une figure qui soit ausi com li fuelle de mirte, si com nos avons conteit, a III oncines desevrez selonc la forme qui est ci:	If a part of the body that is skilled at handling paper requires a large amount of it according to its type, then cut a piece of paper according to the two lines you have written, and start with the largest hairline; and one of the furrows near the natural hair follicles as they grow in thickness, then pull out the root at one of the two angles, then scrape off the entire thing; then sew the two lips together at a stitch of an awl at every thread of fine yarn, and draw out the sinew, and make air to the superfluity of threads on the two spools for any gluans you see this done for; and if not, then leave the stitch and the threads until they have grown three or four; then cure the wound at the costure of things that are dry and constricting, for the paper relaxes from the wound and its assembly, but the costure is dead (as they say the ancients), and it is overwhelming if there is pain; and if in another way: and it is that you see the paper of a figure which is also like the furrow of a mirror, as we have said, at three oncines will follow the form that is here:
puis cope ceu qui sormonte as petites forces igalment selonc la forme qui est ci:	Then comes he who surpasses with equal force according to the form that is here:
Et se tu n’as pooir de tenir les tenailles, et li chose n’est mie igalz, si prent une aguille ou il ait I fil, et la boute emmi la figure; et boute I autre fil delez lou grant larmier, et lou secont fil delez lou petit, et assemble entre tes dois les filz igalment; puis lieve ta main igalment, et lieve tout le cuir sus coi tu as signiet, si com nos avons conteit, puis assemble les II levres de la plaie par costure, et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et se aposteme vient a ton incision, si l’apaise de cerote et de semblans oignement assouajans; et aucune fois avient que li poil de la papiere sont convertit: si covient que tu uses ceu que nos avons dit de l’incision; mais li costure en l’une et en l’autre est plus artificialz.	Then, if you cannot hold the nails, and the thing is not even, take a needle or a thread, and bend the end; and take another thread of the same length for the large garter, and a shorter one for the small, and assemble them correctly between your two hands; then gently press with your hand, and gently sew all the leather where you have made the cut, and close the wound as much as possible; and if the suture comes to your incision, when the pain and swelling are reduced, and no time has come that the paper hair is converted; if you follow what we have said about the incision, but the stitching on both sides is more artificial.
Li cure des caines si est selonc ceste forme: et est que tu convertisses la papiere et la fent dedens selonc ceu que j’ai dit, et puis fai II caines par art, et II liiens subtilz ausi lonc com li papiere et li largesce dou spatumile est; et cope as II chiés de II pars ou tu tiens les filz; puis assemble l’un et l’autre subtilment sus ceu que sormonte de la papiere de l’oil, et estrain les II cainnes des II parties forment; et le laisse ensi aucuns jors, et li cuir qui iert estrainte morra et nercira et porrira, tant qu’il cherra par lui.	The first line of the translation is: "The cure for rabies if it follows this form: and you would convert the paper and make them according to what I have said, then make the rabies by hand, and tie them as subtly as the paper and the long threads are; and cope as the heads of the parts you hold the threads; then assemble one and the other subtly over the paper of the oil, and tighten the rabies in the formed parts; and leave no others, and the leather that is strained will die and turn black and rot, as it will be through it.
S’il tarde, si le cope a unes forces, puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez; et quant li plaie iert soudee, et si ert levee li papiere, et ne poindront plus li poil; et c’est li forme des II cainnes que tu feras selonc ceste figure, et selonc ceste quantiteit de lonc et de large:	If it is late, and the wound has some force, then the care will be as soon as possible; and when the wound is sore, and the paper is lifted, and no more hair is tied; and this is the shape of the two cats that you will make according to this figure, and according to this quantity of long and wide:
li ovraiges est telz que tu preignes une aguille subtil, et i boute I fil de soie souef et subtil; puis assemble les chiés et noe l’un et l’autre subtilment, et soit li longesce des filz une palme de lonc; puis ordene en la chasse I autre fil subtil de soie briément, et noe les chief dou fil; puis mette li malaides son chief en ton sain; et soit delez lou soleil si que li ovraiges soit declairiez, car c’est uns ovraiges subtilz et menus, puis boute l’aguille a tout la chasse en la racine dou poil ajosteit, et la fai percier en la papiere hastanment tant que tu la traies desus lou poil natureil; puis estrai le poil jusque sus la chasse, et boute en la chasse celui poil, s’il en i a I ou II ou III ou plusors; puis estrai ta main tant que li poilz veigne fuers a tout la chasse en la papiere avec lou poil natureil.	The wounds are such that you need a fine needle, and a piece of silk fine and soft; then assemble the heads and knot them gently, and make the length of the threads a palm of length; then order the other fine thread of silk sparingly, and knot the heads of the threads; then place the surgeon's head in your hand; and if the wound is declining, because it is a small wound and thin, then tie the needle all over the course with the hair as loose as possible, and make it perceive on the paper as you drag the natural hair; then pull out the hair until it is through the course, and cut in the course with the hair, if there are one or two or three or more; then pull out your hand as soon as the hair comes all around the course with the natural hair.
Et se li chasse est traite et li poilz ne vient fuer avec li, si trairas la chasse au desoz a tout le fil que tu i as ordeneit, tant que li chasse veigne fuer dou pertus desus et que tu la voies par la vision de l’oil; adonques si trairas la chasse et le fil, et clo l’oil et lou laisse clo II jors ou III, tant que li poil s’aerde en son leu et naisse li char sus; et se li poilz est petis, si acompaigne I poil lonc des chevoulz naturez, et soit alevez avec celui ou tu le laisse, tant qu’il soit eslongiez et puis le lieve.	1. And if the chase is treated and the hair does not come with it, if you trust the chase to the end of the thread that you have ordered, as long as the chase comes out with sharp points and you see it through the oil; therefore, if you trust the chase and the thread, close the oil and leave the thread closed for two or three days, as long as the hair grows in its place and the horn is born; and if the hair is short, then accompany one long hair with the cheeks, as it is longer and then cut it off.
de la porriture de l’oil	2. of the oil's dregs
Quant ceste maladie qui est apelee «aleacrati» ou li porriture vient en l’oil, si en i a de II manieres: l’une natureil, et l’autre innatureil.	When this disease, which is called "aleacrati" or the discharge comes in oil, there are two ways: one natural and the other unnatural.
Et avient par soudement de plaie, ou de tailleure ou de cautere, et par semblans choses.	And it comes from wounds, or cuts, or burns, and in similar ways.
Et li maniere de l’ovraige en li est que tu fendes celle soudure, et dessevre les levres de li, et met dedens tentes de lin, et la lie tant qu’elle soit sanee; et ne covient mie que tu uses en la cure de li de choses que sechent et restraignent.	And the way of the treatment is to cut off the supply, and suck out the poison, and put on dressings of linen, and keep them as long as they are healthy; and nothing else is needed in the cure of it with things that dry and restrict.
Car se tu fais ceu, si revient li maladie pire que li premiere; mais i oevre de choses amollissans, si com fenugreic; et l’arose d’aigue ou altee et semence de lin soient cuites, et oignemens dyaquilon fondut en aucun des oiles, et i envoloupe une tente, et le cure de ceu.	For if you do this, the disease becomes worse than the first; but it works by things that make one weak, like fenugreek; and the rose of ague or altee and the seed of lin are cooked, and all oils are made to dissolve in none of them, and they are wrapped in a tent, and the cure of this.
Et li tresors de ta cure si est que tu te dones en garde qu’ele ne soude mie selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant; et cist ovraiges que nos avons dit nen est fuers que adresemens de ceste maladie, qu’elle ne reviegne selonc la forme qu’elle fut devant.	And the treasures of your cure are if you guard that it does not sound like according to the form it was before; and these ovraiges that we have said, no one has been healed that the disease did not recur according to the form it was before.
de la char qui vient en l’oil	of the care that comes in the oil
Ceste maladie que est desoz qui vraiement est apelee «axacrati», et est naturelz et accidens.	This disease that is called "acaratism" is truly called "acaratism," and it is natural and accidental.
Li accidens vient de plaie et de fendure et de cautere et de choses semblans; et li voie de l’ovraige en li si est que tu preignes un aguille, en coi il ait I fil double, et la fiche en la char, et li fai percier des le senestre larmier tant c’a destre, si que li filz veigne en II chiés de la char; puis estent la char au desus a tout l’aguille, et la cope a I spatumile large.	The accident comes from wounding and bleeding and cauterization and things similar; and the sight of the patient in the mirror is that if you prick with a needle, if it has two fillets, and the thread in the char, and it seems to perceive the left arm as much as the right, so that the threads come in the head of the char; then the char is at the end of all the needle, and the thread in the large spatula.
